like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . very common side effects ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ): infections of the lung ( infection , fever or infection ) infection , including fever or infection ( common ): if you have a temperature of 38ºc or greater , fever or other signs of infection ( since you might have less white blood cells than normal which is very common ). infection ( infection ) may be severe and could lead to fever . if you start feeling chest infection ( signs of a common side effect that may affect up to 1 in 10 , 000 people ). if you experience this side effect , talk to your doctor as soon as possible . reporting of side effects if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
